src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">大济村的明清古民居堪称一绝,它不但雕栏石砌,桥屋相连,而且普遍构筑牌楼式大门,大门曲中见幽,大院前院套后院,大院套小院,每幢房子有6个天井6个天窗,有的甚至有12个天井12个天窗,砖雕木雕石雕,把一幢幢房子装扮得既美观大方又古色古香<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">说大济,最令人不可思议的要算村中的古地道了<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />整个地道网分布在村中约2万平方米的地下,共有7个进出口,分通野外和屋内两式,地道底部用卵石砌面,两壁用平砖错缝纵间叠砌,顶部用若干块扇形拱砖并列砌筑而成拱券,人走进去显得特别幽深和神秘<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />类似小村落的古地道在中国也属罕有<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">而坐落在庆元东部57公里的月山村,相比较大济村而言,除了文化和大济村吴氏一脉相承外,更注重耕读传家<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />这里的吴氏先祖从中原迁徙而来,几经周折,最后落脚在月山村<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />月山村因后山形如半月,村前环水似银钩,状如一轮圆月而得名<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />宋元以来,这里是闽浙通衢官道必经之地,因而人口繁衍,人才辈出,经济发达,店铺林立<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />发展至今,现有人丁1700余人<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">同样崇尚儒学,古时月山村做官的人不少<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />历代来,这个小村名列仕籍者,居然多达200余人,真有点令人难以置信<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />有文化了便派生儒雅,于是, 月山晚翠<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />云泉晓钟<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />龙凤两桥<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />文奎高阁<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />宝塔东耸<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />银屏西峙<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />龙湫灵液<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />虎胜奇岩八景应运而生<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />一个小小的月山村因有了这八景,居住在这里的子民们也便具有了保护环境的文化意识<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />因为文化,小小月山村名声日振,远近的文人墨客们或访亲或休闲纷至沓来,随着时光的推移,这里便成了文化胜地<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">月山村最经典的风景,首屈一指还数古廊桥<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />庆元全县有风格各异的古廊桥97座,月山一个村子就占了10座<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />月山村因有一条举溪又名举水村,在潆洄婉转的举水上,每隔二三十米便耸有一廊桥,故有<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />二里十桥<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" />之美誉<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />而世上构筑技艺最复杂<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />建造年代最久<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />建筑规模最大的木拱古廊桥<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=412384692195414326860672491" />如龙桥<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=540559714740705577652849543" />就坐落在举水之上<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />如龙桥始建于何年已无可考,现为国保文物单位<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />大家都看过美国电影<a target=_blank href="/view/807456.htm"><img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=108932030168486474428289659" />廊桥遗梦<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=881584074518235945079112911" /></a>里的廊桥,彼廊桥与此廊桥相比,实在不值一提,如果有人想在廊桥上浪漫一下的话,还是选择庆元的廊桥为上策<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" <div class="para">主要景点</div><h3 class="headline-2"><a name="7_4" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="sub1041818_7_4" class="anchor-2"></a><a name="特色看点_双门桥" class="anchor-2"></a><span <div class="para">门票<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=820013475104505573524673609" />免费</div><div class="anchor-list"><a name="9" class="anchor-1"></a><a name="sub1041818_9" class="anchor-1"></a><a name="旅游指南" class="anchor-1"></a></div><h2 class="headline-1"><span class="headline-1-index">9</span><span class="headline-content">旅游指南</span><span class="text_edit editable-title" style="margin-left: 10px;" data-edit-id="5742934:%E5%A4%A7%E6%B5%8E%E6%9D%91:9"><a href="#" class="nslog:1019" title="编辑本段">编辑</a></span></h2><div class="para">大济<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />一个偏安于庆元山水之间古村落<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />大济村就位于庆远县城东南二公里<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />在这里<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />人们能见到巧夺天工的明清古屋<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />木屋廊桥<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />接官亭<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />青砖和鹅卵石镶嵌成的金瓷街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />古道等<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />置身其间<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />会误以为是历史时针倒转到了宋明时代<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">大济村</div>
<div class="para">徜徉于村中那些青砖古道<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />明清院落<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />空气中幽幽漂浮的诗书文礼气息让人顿发思古之念<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />看着临清桥头的双桂联坊<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />想起那些平步青云的读书郎如何在这座桥上<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />意气风发地衣锦还乡<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />想来数百年前<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />每遇科举放榜<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />大济总是人声鼎沸<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />鼓乐齐天<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" />而大济迎旨门街<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=327226498813097597389946285" />大济大理相巷等街巷名<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=409173181522516936838209267" />更是传递着曾经的不同凡响<img class="pchar" style="margin-bottom:-3px" src="/wikiui/api/p?c=950481408382793485046963025" /></div>
<div class="para">名门望族</div>
